| NYT | Meeting People | Weather | PHRASE |  | Tá | Yes [to agree with the weather] |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| NYT | Meeting People | Weather | SENTENCE |  | Tá, cinnte. | It is indeed/surely. |  |  |  |  | teh, kintche |  |  |
| NYT | Meeting People | Weather | SENTENCE |  | Tá lá breá ann. | It's a fine day. |  |  |  |  | teh leh breah ann |  |  |

| NYT | Meeting People | Weather | PHRASE |  | Buíochas le Dia | Thank God | Said after “it’s a good day” for example |  |  |  | bwayhas le djia |  | is used quite frequently in this context. |
| NYT | Meeting People | Weather | SENTENCE |  | Tá drochlá ann. | It's a bad day. |  |  |  |  | teh drock-leh ann |  |  |

| NYT | SPEAKING ABOUT YOUR BACKGROUND |  | QUESTION |  | Cá as tú? | Where are you from? |  |  |  |  |  |  | After giving your response, you can ask the same question in the following ways: |

| NYT | Expressing Opinions |  | QUESTION |  | An bhfuil an bia maith? | Is the food any good? |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

| NYT | SAYING WHERE YOU’RE GOING |  | SENTENCE |  | Tá mé ag dul go teach an phobail. | I am going to the church |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| NYT | SAYING WHERE YOU’RE GOING |  | SENTENCE |  | Tá mé ag dul go dtí an t-ospidéal. | I am going to the hospital. |  |  |  |  |  |  | Go dtí is used before nouns that are preceded by the article: |
| NYT | SAYING WHERE YOU’RE GOING |  | SENTENCE |  | Tá mé ag dul abhaile. | I'm going home. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| NYT | SAYING WHERE YOU’RE GOING |  | SENTENCE |  | Tá mé ag dul amach. | I'm going out. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| NYT | SAYING WHERE YOU’RE GOING |  | SENTENCE |  | tá mé ag dul a chodladh | I am going to sleep |  |  |  |  | ...hoh-loo |  |  |
| NYT | SAYING WHERE YOU’RE GOING |  | WORD |  | ansin | then |  |  |  |  |  |  | as in I'm going to ... and then I'm going to... |

| NYT | SAYING WHERE YOU’RE GOING |  | SENTENCE |  | Go Dún Pádraig | To Downpatrick |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

| NYT | SAYING WHERE YOU’RE GOING |  | WORD | GOING_WHEN | i gceann leathuair an chloig | in half an hour |  |  |  |  | i gen le-hoor a clig |  |  |

| NYT | SAYING WHERE YOU’RE GOING |  | WORD |  | uair | an hour |  |  |  |  |  |  | This word occurs quite frequently in everyday speech, so it is well worth learning the different forms. |
| NYT | SAYING WHERE YOU’RE GOING |  | WORD |  | dhá uair | two hours |  |  |  |  |  |  | The word uair is irregular when preceded by numbers: |

## NYT - Taking your leave

| program | topic | topic2 | type | group | irish | meaning | practice_ideas | s_p | m_f | literal_meaning | phonetic | sound | info |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| NYT | Taking your leave |  |  |  | AG FÁGÁIL COMHLUADAIR | TAKING YOUR LEAVE |  |  |  |  | Ag faygal cool-wah-der |  |  |
| NYT | Taking your leave |  |  |  | Caithfidh mé imeacht. | I have to go. |  |  |  |  | Ka-heh meh imackt |  |  |
| NYT | Taking your leave |  |  |  | Caithfidh mé imeacht arís. | I have to go again. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

## NYT - Location and movement 1

| program | topic | topic2 | type | group | irish | meaning | practice_ideas | s_p | m_f | literal_meaning | phonetic | sound | info |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| NYT | Location and movement 1 |  |  |  | Cá bhfuil ...? | Where is/are ...? |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| NYT | Location and movement 1 |  |  |  | Cá bhfuil oifig an phoist? | Where is the post office? |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| NYT | Location and movement 1 |  |  |  | Cá bhfuil do charr? | Where is your car? |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| NYT | Location and movement 1 |  |  |  | Cá bhfuil na heochracha? | Where are the keys? |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| NYT | Location and movement 1 |  |  |  | ... ar chlé | ... on the left |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| NYT | Location and movement 1 |  |  |  | ... ar dheis | ... on the right |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| NYT | Location and movement 1 |  |  |  | Tá sé ansin ar chlé. | It's there on the left. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| NYT | Location and movement 1 |  |  |  | Tá sé anseo ar dheis. | It's here on the right. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| NYT | Location and movement 1 |  |  |  | Tá sé trasna ón siopa. | It's across from the shop. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| NYT | Location and movement 1 |  |  |  | Tá sé in aice leis an chaife. | It's beside the cafe. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| NYT | Location and movement 1 |  |  |  | Cá mhéad seomra atá ann? | How many rooms are in it? |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| NYT | Location and movement 1 |  |  |  | Tá trí sheomra ann. | It has three rooms. |  |  |  |  | If you are not sure why it is trí sheomra but ocht seomra, go back to Unit 6. |  |  |
| NYT | Location and movement 1 |  |  |  | Ocht seomra. | Eight rooms. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| NYT | Location and movement 1 |  |  |  | Téigh suas an staighre. | Go up the stairs. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| NYT | Location and movement 1 |  |  |  | Téigh síos an halla. | Go down the hall. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| NYT | Location and movement 1 |  |  |  | Tiontaigh ... | Turn ... |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| NYT | Location and movement 1 |  |  |  | Tiontaigh ar chlé or ar dheis. | Turn left or right. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| NYT | Location and movement 1 |  |  |  | an chéad doras ar chlé | the first door on the left |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| NYT | Location and movement 1 |  |  |  | an chéad | the first |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
